	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Curaçao</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about the island country. For the former colony/territory comprising Curaçao and five other islands, see <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao_and_Dependencies" title="Curaçao and Dependencies">Curaçao and Dependencies</a>. For the liqueur, see <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao_(liqueur)" title="Curaçao (liqueur)">Curaçao (liqueur)</a>.</div><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Not to be confused with <a href="/wiki/Curacoa_(disambiguation)" class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" title="Curacoa (disambiguation)">Curacoa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Curassow" title="Curassow">Curassow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Carriacou" title="Carriacou">Carriacou</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Curu%C3%A7%C3%A1_River_(Javari_River)" title="Curuçá River (Javari River)">Curuçá River (Javari River)</a>.</div>
<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Island country in the Caribbean, part of the Kingdom of the Netherlands</div>

Antillean guilder">Netherlands Antillean guilder</a> (<a href="/wiki/ISO_4217" title="ISO 4217">ANG</a>)</td></tr><tr class="mergedtoprow"><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Time_zone" title="Time zone">Time zone</a></th><td><a href="/wiki/UTC-4:00" class="mw-redirect" title="UTC-4:00">UTC-4:00</a> (<a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Time_Zone" title="Atlantic Time Zone">AST</a>)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Left-_and_right-hand_traffic" title="Left- and right-hand traffic">Driving side</a></th><td>right</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Telephone_numbers_in_Cura%C3%A7ao" class="mw-redirect" title="Telephone numbers in Curaçao">Calling code</a></th><td><a href="/wiki/Telephone_numbers_in_Cura%C3%A7ao_and_the_Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Telephone numbers in Curaçao and the Caribbean Netherlands">+599</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166" title="ISO 3166">ISO 3166 code</a></th><td><div class="hlist hlist-separated"><ul><li><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-2:CW" title="ISO 3166-2:CW">CW</a></li><li><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-2:NL" title="ISO 3166-2:NL">NL-CW</a></li></ul></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Country_code_top-level_domain" title="Country code top-level domain">Internet TLD</a></th><td><a href="/wiki/.cw" title=".cw">.cw</a></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Curaçao</b> (<span class="nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="&#39;k&#39; in &#39;kind&#39;">k</span><span title="/jʊər/: &#39;ure&#39; in &#39;cure&#39;">jʊər</span><span title="/ə/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;about&#39;">ə</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/oʊ/: &#39;o&#39; in &#39;code&#39;">oʊ</span></span>, <wbr />-<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/aʊ/: &#39;ou&#39; in &#39;mouth&#39;">aʊ</span></span>, <wbr /><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˌ/: secondary stress follows">ˌ</span><span title="&#39;k&#39; in &#39;kind&#39;">k</span><span title="/jʊər/: &#39;ure&#39; in &#39;cure&#39;">jʊər</span><span title="/ə/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;about&#39;">ə</span><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/oʊ/: &#39;o&#39; in &#39;code&#39;">oʊ</span></span>, <wbr />-<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/aʊ/: &#39;ou&#39; in &#39;mouth&#39;">aʊ</span></span>/</a></span></span> <a href="/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i title="English pronunciation respelling"><span style="font-size:90%">KEWR</span>-əss-oh, -&#8288;ow, -&#8288;<span style="font-size:90%">OH</span>, -&#8288;<span style="font-size:90%">OW</span></i></a>,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> <small>Dutch:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Dutch" title="Help:IPA/Dutch">[kyraːˈsʌu, kur-]</a></span>&#32;<span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nl-Cura%C3%A7ao.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/01/Nl-Cura%C3%A7ao.ogg" class="internal" title="Nl-Curaçao.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span>;<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Papiamento_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Papiamento language">Papiamento</a>: <i lang="pap">Kòrsou</i> <small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA" title="Help:IPA">[ˈkɔrsɔu̯]</a></span>) is a <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">Lesser Antilles</a> island in the southern <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">Caribbean Sea</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Dutch_Caribbean" title="Dutch Caribbean">Dutch Caribbean</a> region, about 65&#160;km (40&#160;mi) north of the <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> coast. It is a constituent country (<a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">Dutch</a>: <i lang="nl">land</i>) of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The country was formerly part of the <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao_and_Dependencies" title="Curaçao and Dependencies">Curaçao and Dependencies</a> colony in 1815–1954 and later the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_Antilles" title="Netherlands Antilles">Netherlands Antilles</a> in 1954–2010, as "Island Territory of Curaçao"<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> (Dutch: <i lang="nl">Eilandgebied Curaçao</i>, Papiamento: <i lang="pap">Teritorio Insular di Kòrsou</i>) and is now formally called the <b>Country of Curaçao</b> (Dutch: <i lang="nl">Land Curaçao</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Papiamento: <i lang="pap">Pais Kòrsou</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> It includes the main island of Curaçao and the much smaller, uninhabited island of <a href="/wiki/Klein_Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Klein Curaçao">Klein Curaçao</a> ("Little Curaçao").<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Curaçao has a population of 149,600 (July 2017 est.)<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> and an area of 444&#160;km<sup>2</sup> (171&#160;sq&#160;mi); its capital is <a href="/wiki/Willemstad" title="Willemstad">Willemstad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
